#### 09-Aug-2024 (Friday)
* <details> <summary><strong>Languages: </strong>(Class 3) More on Phonetics</summary>
 
  * [3. ClassNotes.pdf](1.%20Languages/4.%20AllLangugages/3.%20ClassNotes-09082024-Lan.pdf)  
  * Video  
  * **Verified HW Solutions:** 
	* [3. HW_09082024_Phonetics.pdf](1.%20Languages/4.%20AllLangugages/3.%20HW_09082024_Phonetics.pdf)
	* [3.PhoneticAlphabet-IPA-09082024.xlsx](1.%20Languages/4.%20AllLangugages/3.PhoneticAlphabet-IPA-09082024.xlsx)  
  * **Details:** 
    1. Continued Shri Mataji’s lecture from yesterday  
    2. Phonetics:  
    3. Correct phonetic chart - aha am .. need to be ‘aɱ’ and ‘aɦ’.. because we can also have ‘iɱ’ and ‘iɦ’, or ‘uɱ’ and ‘uɦ’... may be better not to use aⁿ aʰ as we are using half h for bha, kha etc which in chandassu are not samyultakshars.. but am and aha are themselves guru sounds..  
    4. Fill rest of phonetic chart for English language like in  
    5. [https://www.oxfordlearnersdictionaries.com/us/about/english/pronunciation\_english](https://www.oxfordlearnersdictionaries.com/us/about/english/pronunciation_english)  
    6. English text to Phonetics: [https://tophonetics.com/](https://tophonetics.com/)  
    7. IPA English alphabet: [https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA/English](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA/English)  
    8. Chandassu check homework and do a couple more examples - more complicated ones like utpalamaala, champakamaala etc.  
    9. Chandassu for one telugu poem with more complex ganas  
    10. Chandassu for one Carnatic music song
</details>

    1. Select a project: Waves and Music

       1. Poster summary :

       1. Be confident and loud (don't be shy (left sided) don't be arrogant (right sided))  
       2. Describe everything in a way anyone can understand even if they don’t know anything about your project before  
       3. Present everything quickly but nicely  
       4. Practice your presentation for several times  
       5. Describe everything in your own words (don't just read what's on the poster).

       2. Practice presenting your project story and answering questions

The presentation will be on the topic of "Waves & Music", and will use programming to demonstrate how waves work and their relation to musical notes. The presentation will include a demonstration of how sound waves can be generated using a flute and a piano. The students will use Python libraries to create functions for generating musical notes and waves. They will also show how different properties of waves, such as amplitude, frequency, and velocity, can be controlled to create different musical sounds.

Print Google Maps results for each country and compare them to the Python map output. (Zoom out and compare). (Use Alt+Tab to switch between applications on Windows operating systems)  
   5. AI Summary of maps for an 8-year-old  
   6. HW: Study and memorize this summary.  
   7. AI Homework exercises on maps  
   8. HW: Finish the exercises and ask your parents to correct them.  
   9. HW: Play with Python code: "1.3D Globe.py", "3. 3D Globe Earth map offline.py" (May have to install packages in the terminal using: \`pip install geopandas requests bs4\`)
